\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{00001\ \textcolor{comment}{/**********************************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00002\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00003\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ raylib\ -\/\ A\ simple\ and\ easy-\/to-\/use\ library\ to\ enjoy\ videogames\ programming\ (www.raylib.com)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00004\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00005\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ FEATURES:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00006\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ NO\ external\ dependencies,\ all\ required\ libraries\ included\ with\ raylib}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00007\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ Multiplatform:\ Windows,\ Linux,\ FreeBSD,\ OpenBSD,\ NetBSD,\ DragonFly,\ MacOS,\ UWP,\ Android,\ Raspberry\ Pi,\ HTML5.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00008\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ Written\ in\ plain\ C\ code\ (C99)\ in\ PascalCase/camelCase\ notation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00009\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ Hardware\ accelerated\ with\ OpenGL\ (1.1,\ 2.1,\ 3.3\ or\ ES2\ -\/\ choose\ at\ compile)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00010\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ Unique\ OpenGL\ abstraction\ layer\ (usable\ as\ standalone\ module):\ [rlgl]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00011\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ Multiple\ Fonts\ formats\ supported\ (TTF,\ XNA\ fonts,\ AngelCode\ fonts)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00012\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ Outstanding\ texture\ formats\ support,\ including\ compressed\ formats\ (DXT,\ ETC,\ ASTC)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00013\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ Full\ 3d\ support\ for\ 3d\ Shapes,\ Models,\ Billboards,\ Heightmaps\ and\ more!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00014\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ Flexible\ Materials\ system,\ supporting\ classic\ maps\ and\ PBR\ maps}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00015\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ Skeletal\ Animation\ support\ (CPU\ bones-\/based\ animation)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00016\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ Shaders\ support,\ including\ Model\ shaders\ and\ Postprocessing\ shaders}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00017\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ Powerful\ math\ module\ for\ Vector,\ Matrix\ and\ Quaternion\ operations:\ [raymath]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00018\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ Audio\ loading\ and\ playing\ with\ streaming\ support\ (WAV,\ OGG,\ MP3,\ FLAC,\ XM,\ MOD)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00019\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ VR\ stereo\ rendering\ with\ configurable\ HMD\ device\ parameters}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00020\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ Bindings\ to\ multiple\ programming\ languages\ available!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00021\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00022\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ NOTES:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00023\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ One\ custom\ font\ is\ loaded\ by\ default\ when\ InitWindow()\ [core]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00024\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ If\ using\ OpenGL\ 3.3\ or\ ES2,\ one\ default\ shader\ is\ loaded\ automatically\ (internally\ defined)\ [rlgl]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00025\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ If\ using\ OpenGL\ 3.3\ or\ ES2,\ several\ vertex\ buffers\ (VAO/VBO)\ are\ created\ to\ manage\ lines-\/triangles-\/quads}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00026\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00027\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ DEPENDENCIES\ (included):}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00028\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ [core]\ rglfw\ (github.com/glfw/glfw)\ for\ window/context\ management\ and\ input\ (only\ PLATFORM\_DESKTOP)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00029\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ [rlgl]\ glad\ (github.com/Dav1dde/glad)\ for\ OpenGL\ 3.3\ extensions\ loading\ (only\ PLATFORM\_DESKTOP)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00030\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ [raudio]\ miniaudio\ (github.com/dr-\/soft/miniaudio)\ for\ audio\ device/context\ management}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00031\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00032\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ OPTIONAL\ DEPENDENCIES\ (included):}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00033\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ [core]\ rgif\ (Charlie\ Tangora,\ Ramon\ Santamaria)\ for\ GIF\ recording}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00034\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ [textures]\ stb\_image\ (Sean\ Barret)\ for\ images\ loading\ (BMP,\ TGA,\ PNG,\ JPEG,\ HDR...)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00035\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ [textures]\ stb\_image\_write\ (Sean\ Barret)\ for\ image\ writting\ (BMP,\ TGA,\ PNG,\ JPG)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00036\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ [textures]\ stb\_image\_resize\ (Sean\ Barret)\ for\ image\ resizing\ algorithms}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00037\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ [textures]\ stb\_perlin\ (Sean\ Barret)\ for\ Perlin\ noise\ image\ generation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00038\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ [text]\ stb\_truetype\ (Sean\ Barret)\ for\ ttf\ fonts\ loading}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00039\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ [text]\ stb\_rect\_pack\ (Sean\ Barret)\ for\ rectangles\ packing}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00040\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ [models]\ par\_shapes\ (Philip\ Rideout)\ for\ parametric\ 3d\ shapes\ generation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00041\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ [models]\ tinyobj\_loader\_c\ (Syoyo\ Fujita)\ for\ models\ loading\ (OBJ,\ MTL)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00042\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ [models]\ cgltf\ (Johannes\ Kuhlmann)\ for\ models\ loading\ (glTF)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00043\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ [raudio]\ stb\_vorbis\ (Sean\ Barret)\ for\ OGG\ audio\ loading}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00044\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ [raudio]\ dr\_flac\ (David\ Reid)\ for\ FLAC\ audio\ file\ loading}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00045\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ [raudio]\ dr\_mp3\ (David\ Reid)\ for\ MP3\ audio\ file\ loading}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00046\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ [raudio]\ jar\_xm\ (Joshua\ Reisenauer)\ for\ XM\ audio\ module\ loading}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00047\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ [raudio]\ jar\_mod\ (Joshua\ Reisenauer)\ for\ MOD\ audio\ module\ loading}}
